# Active context вҖ” focus Д‘ang chбәЎy

> **File "Д‘ang б»ҹ Д‘Гўu"** (volatile, Д‘б»•i liГӘn tб»Ҙc). `session-start` echo ~3000 byte Д‘бә§u khi mб»ҹ phiГӘn В·
> `pre-compact` ghim lГ m "plan sб»‘ng" В· `verify-before-stop` nhбәҜc cбәӯp nhбәӯt khi Д‘б»•i >1 file source. Giб»Ҝ phбә§n
> load-bearing (Focus В· Next В· Ledger) **gбә§n Д‘бә§u file**. ДҗГўy **khГҙng** phбәЈi nguб»“n chГўn lГҪ вҖ” chб»ү scratchpad phб»‘i
> hб»Јp; muб»‘n binding phбәЈi thГ nh ADR/luбәӯt (`agent-harness.md` В§Ranh giб»ӣi promote memory).

**(archived 2026-07-16 sГЎng): FILAMENT-COLOUR EPIC вҖ” f-5 SPRITE PER-PART COLOUR (Track A) BUILT + VERIFIED off-box** on `feat/f5-sprite-part-colors` (off `main` `a46c883` = f-2-click **PR #142 MERGED**). **The sprite_render turntable now paints each named part in its DEFAULT filament colour.** Server-computed вҶ’ **NO openapi/sqlc/migration/codegen.** **Flow:** core-api `CreateProductAssetJob` (sprite only) builds a `{objectName вҶ’ "#RRGGBB"}` snapshot via new pure `spritePartColors(parts,colors)` вҖ” first AVAILABLE colour per mapped part in catalog order (D-C; colours have no display_order, `ListColorsByProduct` sorts by name = editor/storefront order), hex re-validated `#RRGGBB` at the render boundary (D-E, `hexColorRe`; malformed вҶ’ 400, never a grey part; unmapped/uncoloured part omitted) вҶ’ frozen into the `asset_job.created` payload (`assetJobCreatedPayload.PartColors`, `omitempty` вҶ’ model_ingest & uncoloured-sprite wire **byte-identical**, ADR-006 idempotent snapshot). Worker: `job.rs AssetJob.part_colors` (`#[serde(default)]`); `sprite_render.rs` serializes вҶ’ `render.rs` sets env **`LUMIN_PART_COLORS`** (inherits render.py вҶ’ Blender, keeps render.py's arg contract stable, dodges shell-quoting VN names); `_bl_render.py` matches `o.data.name`(mesh)/`o.name`(node) вҶ’ Principled Base Color; NEW `_color.py` (bpy-free, self-checked) does **sRGBвҶ’linear** (Base Color is linear; raw sRGB renders too dark). **NOT [MONEY]** (render colour only; checkout/pricing/`part_colors` untouched). **Amends ADR-049** (payload grows partColors; first-colour default + manual re-render are "within ADR-049"). **VERIFIED off-box:** Go build/vet/**golangci 0**/gofmt + `spritePartColors` unit + **real-PG** (`TestCreateAssetJobFreezesPartColors`: sprite payload freezes partColors, model_ingest omits via omitempty) + existing e2e green; Rust **41 tests** (2 new part_colors wire) + clippy -D + fmt; py **`_color` self-check** + py_compile Г—3. **BOX-GATED (o-1c) вҖ” the GPU render only:** on the GTX-1060 box render a sprite for a mapped multi-object product вҶ’ confirm each part shows its filament colour + Blender object names match the mapped `model_object_name` (correct-by-construction off-box). **вң… MERGED PR #143 (main `443d354`); ADR-049 amendment landed via valve.** **рҹҺү FILAMENT-COLOUR EPIC FULLY DONE & ON MAIN** вҖ” f-1 #138 В· f-2 dropdown #139 + click #142 В· f-4 #140 В· f-3 #141 В· f-5 #143. **Only OPS steps remain to light it up in prod (NOT code):** (1) re-ingest existing products (structured glb + object-name list + named materials all post-date them); (2) on the GTX-1060 box, render a sprite for a MAPPED multi-object product вҶ’ confirm each part shows its filament colour + Blender object names match `model_object_name` (o-1c box-gate, see [[lumin-phase5-deploy-env]]).

Then gltf-transform LOD compression + sprite_render (Blender/GPU) are the remaining follow-ups.

**вһЎпёҸ (DONE) PHASE 5 вҖ” ASSET-WORKER CONSUMER SPINE (Rust) вҶ’ PR #128 MERGED** (`main` `c1eee74`; was off `59661f7` = #127 MERGED). The workerвҶ’ side of ADR-045. Durable JetStream **WorkQueue** pull consumer over `ASSET_JOBS` binds `asset_job.created` (concurrency=1) вҶ’ processвҶ’reportвҶ’ack lifecycle (at-least-once В· InProgress heartbeat В· DLQ on max-deliver) вҶ’ reports each result to core-api via `PATCH /internal/asset-jobs/{id}` (the endpoint #127 built). **Actual per-kind processing is a SEAM** (`processor::Processor`): binary wires `Unimplemented` (every job вҶ’ Transient вҶ’ redeliver вҶ’ nothing consumed/failed) so an early deploy is safe. **Key insight: `model_ingest` is CPU (trimesh/gltf-transform), only `sprite_render` is GPU (Blender)** вҖ” so this spine + the real model_ingest are NOT GPU-gated; only sprite_render + the Dockerfile tooling truly need the box. **Files (5 new + 4 edit):** NEW `job.rs`(payload, camelCase, pins Go `assetJobCreatedPayload`)/`processor.rs`(trait+Unimplemented)/`callback.rs`(Reporter+HttpReporter, camelCase body, omit-none)/`pipeline.rs`(pure `decide`+`handle_job`)/ В· EDIT `config.rs`(+stream/durable/max_deliver/ack_wait/heartbeat/core_api_url/token) В· `worker.rs`(consumer loop + heartbeat + settle) В· `main.rs`(mods) В· `Cargo.toml`(+serde/serde_json/reqwest-rustls/futures) В· `asset-worker.yaml`(CORE_API_URL+WORKER_CALLBACK_TOKEN real env, optional:true) В· README. **verify:** `make verify-rs` GREEN (fmt В· clippy -D warnings В· **16 tests**: parseГ—3, callback-serializeГ—2, configГ—4, decideГ—4, handle_jobГ—3 incl. report-failureвҶ’nak idempotency). **NOT built (next slice, tooling/GPU-gated):** real `model_ingest` (trimesh normalize + gltf-transform LOD glb + S3 fetch/upload) + `sprite_render` (Blender) + Dockerfile trimesh/gltf/sharp tooling + Garage upload creds. **Live NATS bind+drain = deploy smoke** (documented, like o-1c Blender check) вҖ” unit-tested logic + compile-verified binding, not run against real JetStream here.

**вһЎпёҸ (DONE) PHASE 5 вҖ” GPU DEVICE-PLUGIN + ASSET-PIPELINE OUTPUT CALLBACK (core-api side) вҶ’ PR #127 MERGED** (`main` `59661f7`). Two deliverables, ADR-045.
**(A) GPU device-plugin** вҖ” the scheduling blocker, not pipeline code: `asset-worker.yaml` requests `nvidia.com/gpu: 1` but nothing advertises it вҶ’ Pending forever. NEW `infra/k8s/nvidia-device-plugin.yaml` = NVIDIA's canonical static DaemonSet (kube-system), pinned `v0.14.5`, +2 box deltas: `runtimeClassName: nvidia` (plugin's NVML probe only sees the GTX 1060 under the nvidia runtime вҖ” k3s doesn't default it) + `FAIL_ON_INIT_ERROR=false` (idle not crashloop). Wired: README runbook step 7 + В§GPU-prerequisite + `operations.md В§3` step 3b.
**(B) Output callback (workerвҶ’core-apiвҶ’Product)** вҖ” user chose **authenticated endpoint** + **build the verifiable slice** (ADR-045). `PATCH /internal/asset-jobs/{id}` (`ReportAssetJobResult`): 3rd auth realm **`authService`** (static `WORKER_CALLBACK_TOKEN` bearer, constant-time, **fail-closed** when unset), row-locked idempotent tx (`FOR UPDATE`; `ready` terminal+sticky), a `ready model_ingest` writes `products.model3d_url` (**D3** вҖ” the one writer `UpdateProduct` never touches), output URL **host-pinned** to assets origin + `.glb` (`modelstore.OwnsOutputURL` вҖ” it becomes a client-side `<model-viewer src>`). Fixed latent trap: worker `config.rs` default subject `asset.job` вҶ’ real `asset_job.created` on WorkQueue `ASSET_JOBS`. Files: openapi+regen В· config/server/main wiring В· middleware_auth authService В· sqlc `GetAssetJobByIDForUpdate`+`SetProductModel3dUrl`+regen В· `internal_asset_jobs.go` В· core-api.yaml env optional:true + secret.example + asset-worker.yaml reserve-comment.
**verify:** cargo fmt/clippy/3 green В· **`make verify-go` GREEN** (golangci 0 В· sqlc vet/diff В· oapi stale В· `-race` incl. new auth-gate Docker-free + testcontainer integration [ready/sticky/failed/processing/missing-url-400/foreign-url-400/unknown-404]) В· manifest YAML parses (kubectl apply + Blender GPU check are BOX-gated, not runnable on this Mac).
**Render PIPELINE (Rust consumer + Blender/CUDA + trimesh + Garage upload) deliberately NOT built** вҖ” box-gated (GTX 1060, o-1c "Blender sees GPU in-container" unrunnable here). `sprite_render` output still deferred (no storefront consumer; model-viewer loads the `.glb`). **NEXT (on the box): Rust WorkQueue consumer binds `ASSET_JOBS`/`asset_job.created` вҶ’ dispatch model_ingest (trimesh normalize + glb LOD) вҶ’ upload glb to lumin-assets вҶ’ call the callback with `WORKER_CALLBACK_TOKEN`; wire CORE_API_URL+token into asset-worker.yaml.**

**вһЎпёҸ (DONE/superseded) PHASE 4 e-4 FOLLOW-UP (Extension toolbar quick-actions popup)** (`feat/p4-e4-toolbar-popup` off `main` `9bf0c0d` = e-4 templates #114 MERGED). **Un-defers the toolbar popup** the e-4 templates slice scope-cut. **FE-only, no BE/openapi/api-client, money-FREE.** MV3 `action.default_popup: 'popup.html'` вҶ’ toolbar icon opens a 3-button launcher (TбәЎo Д‘ЖЎn / Tra cб»©u / Mбә«u deep-links). onChanged is the race safety-net). **Shared `lib/tabs.ts`** = `Tab`/`TABS`/`isLaunchTab` guard/`LAUNCH_KEY` вҖ” ONE source for popup buttons + shell tabs (no drift); `isLaunchTab` rejects stale/tampered storage вҶ’ UI state. **Trade (documented in `manifest.config.ts` note):** `default_popup` REPLACES the former 1-click-to-panel (costs 1 extra click to reach panel, but lands on the right screen) вҶ’ **DELETED `background.ts`** (its only job = `openPanelOnActionClick`, now the popup's) + removed `background` manifest key. `LAUNCH_KEY` deliberately NOT cleared = "remember last screen" (guardian NOTE, harmless/guarded, no change). **ADR-011 clean BY CONSTRUCTION:** popup only deep-links вҖ” NO chat scan, NO domain/active-tab-URL read, NO host_permissions added (still core-api origin only), NO content scripts; `chrome.windows.getCurrent` needs no perm (only `.url` would). **Files (5 new + 4 edit):** NEW `popup.html`/`src/popup-main.tsx`/`src/screens/popup.tsx`/`src/lib/tabs.ts`/`test/tabs.test.ts` В· EDIT `manifest.config.ts`(+default_popup вҲ’background) В· `screens/shell.tsx`(import TABS from lib/tabs + launchTab effect + fix stale "coming soon" comment) В· `i18n/vi.ts`(+`popup.subtitle`) В· `vite.config.ts`(comment) В· DELETE `src/background.ts`. **verify:** ext typecheck/lint/**32 test**(2 new tabs)/CRXJS-build (dist emits `popup.html`+chunk; frozen `costSnapshot` breakdown + biГӘn per-line; honors 4c-2 oracle carry-forwards #1-4] вҶ’ **Stage 4 DONE**) В· в‘ӨFE editor **STARTED** (**l-1 core Product CRUD MERGED #89** [fill 2 dead seam P3-k; **Stage 2 sub-PRs:** **2a** catalog model вң… **MERGED #76** (`main` `fd144e3`) В· **2b split (money path):** **2b-1** pricing (`Selection`+3 invariants+`PriceItem`, PURE) вң… **MERGED #77** (`main` `c69222c`) В· **2b-2** capture+wire вң… **MERGED #78** (`main` `2c902b5`) В· **2c** storefront consume (part-grouped colors+choice options+cart key) вң… **MERGED #79** (`main` `accc38c`) В· **2d** admin order-detail + print read (denormalize-at-capture per ADR-037 pt 2) вң… BUILT+VERIFIED (reviews next) В· Stage 2 = DONE after 2d.

**вҖ” Stage 4 = P3-s Vбәӯt tЖ° & chi phГӯ (GREENFIELD costing engine) вҖ” ADR-039 written, user chose FULL engine вҖ”**
**Design fork resolved:** design (Admin screen 8) = full COGS engine (weighted-avg filament batches В· mГЎy khбәҘu hao В· phб»Ҙ phГўn-bб»• В· hao-hб»Ҙt 30d В· **snapshot giГЎ vб»‘n chб»‘t-lГәc-bГЎn** В· deduct-on-print). **BUILT + VERIFIED.** The money-freeze slice: when a print job **first** enters PRINTING, deduct-on-print (4b) already froze the filament cost in-tx; a **best-effort post-commit** rollup reads that back + mГЎy/hao-hб»Ҙt/phб»Ҙ and freezes the **whole COGS** onto `order_items.cost_snapshot`. **Design-anchored:** `db.ComputeCostSnapshot` reproduces the design card (screen 8) **вӮ«119,178** exactly вҖ” filament вӮ«77,868 + mГЎy (6.5hГ—вӮ«2,380) вӮ«15,470 + **hao-hб»Ҙt (8.4% of filament+machine) вӮ«7,840** [waste base = filament+machine, NOT aux вҖ” decoded from the card arithmetic] + phб»Ҙ вӮ«18,000. **Migration 000021** `order_items.cost_snapshot` **jsonb NULLABLE** (NULL="chЖ°a chб»‘t" вҖ” oracle R1: a starved print [0g drawn, no ledger row] still writes snapshot filamentVnd=0, NOT NULL вҶ’ margin never inflated) + `products.est_print_minutes` (int additive DEFAULT 0; **wire=`estPrintHours` giб»қ**, handler Д‘б»•i giб»қГ—60 = **phГәt chГӯnh xГЎc** вҶ’ money-freeze dГ№ng big.Rat exact, KHГ”NG float, KHГ”NG pgtype.Numeric [no numeric precedent in repo]). **`db/costing_snapshot.go`:** `ComputeCostSnapshot` (PURE вҖ” machineVnd=estMinГ—purchaseГ·(60Г—monthsГ—hours), wasteVnd=(filament+machine)Г—scrapГ·print, auxVnd=ОЈper_order+ОЈper_monthГ·realOrders30d, all **`ratToVND` round-once** reused from 4b; guards no-machine/print=0/0-orders) + `SnapshotOrderItem` (reads `ItemCostInputs` [ОЈ frozen consumption per item вҖ” **oracle R2 SUM, read frozen cost, never re-derive** + est_min join] + `SnapshotShopInputs` [scrap/print 30d + aux totals + realOrders30d, ONE round-trip] + `PrimaryMachine` [`is_primary AND active ORDER BY updated_at DESC LIMIT 1` вҖ” **spec-guardian 4c-1 NOTE tiebreak**], marshal `db.CostSnapshot`, write; **best-effort**) + `Summary` (KPI, shares `auxPerOrderVnd`/`wasteFactorFloat` helpers). **Seam:** `AdvancePrintJobStage` вҖ” post-commit (after `printHub.broadcast`), only when claimedNow, `db.NewCosting(s.pool).SnapshotOrderItem` best-effort (errвҶ’`logger.Warn`, cost_snapshot NULL, backfill; **never fails move / blocks board / cascades onto paid order**). **est capture:** `cleanProductInput` +estPrintHours (NaN/Inf/<0/>1000h вҶ’ 400; hoursвҶ’minutes round) вҶ’ Insert/UpdateProduct; `productDTO` +estPrintHours (minutesвҶ’hours, 0 omitted). **read-back:** `orderItemsDTO` +`costSnapshotDTO` (jsonbвҶ’api.CostSnapshot, omit-when-NULL вҶ’ flat/uncosted line byte-identical). **KPI:** `GET /admin/costing-summary` (owner+staff default; wasteFactor/auxPerOrderVnd/realOrders30d/primaryMachineVndPerHour? вҖ” **realOrders30d = `payment_confirmed_at вүҘ now()вҲ’30d AND status<>'REFUNDED'`, khб»ӣp dashboard.sql net-revenue predicate** вҶ’ biГӘn khб»ӣp dashboard). **openapi** +CostSnapshot/CostingSummary schemas + OrderItem.costSnapshot (read-only optional) + Product/ProductInput.estPrintHours (optional, no `default:` вҶ’ optional TS, no ripple [[lumin-openapi-default-makes-ts-required]]) + `GET /admin/costing-summary`; regen api.gen.go + schema.gen.ts **staged**. **classify** GetCostingSummary вҶ’ authRequired (read default, pinned in test). **NO** new dep В· **NO** customer money-path (giГЎ vб»‘n/biГӘn tГЎch khб»Ҹi `PriceItem`) В· **NO** FE (4d). **Verify ALL GREEN:** `make verify-go` EXIT=0 (golangci **0** В· gofmt/vet В· sqlc/oapi stale **staged** В· `go test -race` incl real-PG **`TestCostSnapshotEndToEnd`** [вҶ’PRINTING вҶ’ snapshot вӮ«95550 (58500+12000+7050+18000), DTO read-back, `GET /admin/costing-summary` waste 0.1/aux 18000/вӮ«h 2000] + **`TestCostSnapshotNoPrimaryMachine`** [machineVnd 0, still non-NULL] + db 56s / httpapi 64s) В· Docker-free **`db.TestComputeCostSnapshot`** [design вӮ«119,178 + 6 guards] + **`httpapi.TestCostSnapshotDTO`** [JSON-tag alignment] + `TestCleanProductInput` +estPrintHours + classify pin В· `pnpm verify` **6/6** (schema.stale regen-match В· storefront 185 В· prettier) В· storefront+admin typecheck direct cold (optional additive вҶ’ no ripple). **acceptance Cб»Ҙm 46 `ADM-22` Go-gated `[ ]`.** **вң… spec-guardian PASS (0 BLK/0 WARN/1 NOTE)** вҖ” NOTE = ADR-039 В§Hб»Ү quбәЈ *prose* lags impl by one field (`est_print_hours`вҶ’stored `est_print_minutes`; snapshot landed 000021 not sketched-000019); binding decisions honored, "no new ADR needed" (offer valve-sync as follow-up). **вң… ORACLE "design holds"** (clean money-freeze; R1/R2/is_primary honored; overflow-safe big.Int.Mul; post-commit never cascades onto paid order; exactly-one-rollup-per-claim; 3 approximations acceptable). **Oracle 4d (FE) carry-forwards:** (1) NULL `cost_snapshot` = distinct "chЖ°a chб»‘t" empty state, **NOT вӮ«0 margin** (R1 read-side trap); (2) render frozen rates (`estPrintHours`/`machineVndPerHour`/`wasteFactor`) **FROM the blob**, don't recompute from live machines/aux (drift defeats the freeze); (3) multi-item order aux over-counts per line вҖ” surface per-line/note caveat if aggregating order-level margin; (4) money int-VND via the single `packages/core` formatter, no `toLocaleString` in the card. **NEXT: commit вҶ’ push вҶ’ PR вҶ’ user gate; then 4d.**

filter/search miss вҶ’ "khГҙng khб»ӣp" + "Bб»Ҹ lб»Қc" reset (no dead-end). **a11y KHOГҒ:** primary CTA uses `bg-primary`/`text-on-primary` (theme resolves flame700 #C93A1A 5.12:1), **NOT** design's white-on-flame-500 (2.82:1 FAIL AA). **"+ ThГӘm" = header button** (matches hi-fi screen 4 top-right; plan said "FAB" but design shows a header pill вҖ” desktop-first, responsive; `ponytail:` floating mobile FAB skipped). **Seams for P3-l (dead links until then, P3-c precedent):** cardвҶ’`/san-pham/{id}`, header/empty CTAвҶ’`/san-pham/moi`. **FE role N/A** (read-only, no owner/staff branch; **вҖ” P3-h history (MERGED #70 вҶ’ `main` `d2d2f1b`) вҖ”**
**рҹ”Ё PHASE 3 В· P3-h (FE `/hang-doi-in` kanban kГ©o-thбәЈ + SSE live вҖ” print board) вҖ” BUILT + VERIFIED on `feat/phase-3-admin-p3h-print-board`**

the client `<PrintBoard>` keeps it live. **KEY DESIGN вҖ” SSE reaches core-api via a same-origin proxy, NOT a direct cross-origin EventSource:** `CORE_API_URL`
is server-only (never `NEXT_PUBLIC`) + the `lumin_session` cookie is httpOnly on the admin host, so the browser CANNOT open an EventSource straight at
core-api. New route handler `app/api/print-stream/route.ts` (Node runtime, `force-dynamic`) reads the cookie server-side and pipes core-api's
`/admin/print-queue/stream` back **byte-for-byte** (returns `upstream.body` ReadableStream вҖ” no buffering; `request.signal` forwarded so a browser disconnect
tears down the upstream вҶ’ core-api `ctx.Done`). This is the concrete meaning of P3-g's "EventSource same-origin" comment. GET (initial board) + PATCH (drag)
stay **Server Actions** (server-side, cookie-forward) вҖ” only the ONE streaming endpoint needs the proxy. **Drag = @dnd-kit** (`@dnd-kit/core@6.3.1`, 1 new
dep, D-P3-8) вҖ” MouseSensor 8px + TouchSensor hold-200ms (so a mobile swipe still scrolls; no `touch-action:none` trap); **only `listeners` spread, NOT
`attributes`** вҶ’ the card stays a plain container and the accessible control is the per-card **"Chuyб»ғn sang {stage}" button** (keyboard/AT/mobile path,
D-P3-2 вҖ” avoids nesting a real button inside a role=button). **STAGE-ONLY (D6):** both drag + button `PATCH /admin/print-jobs/{id}` move **only print_jobs.stage**,
they do **NOT** transition OrderStatus вҖ” the design's "kГ©o вҶ’ tб»ұ Д‘б»•i trбәЎng thГЎi khГЎch" is intentionally decoupled (order status goes through the P3-e transition
flow with the QC/tracking gate a board drag must never bypass); dropped the design's "Дҗбә¶T TRбә NG THГҒI KHГҒCH" legend as factually wrong for our contract.
**Optimistic:** card moves immediately вҶ’ reconciles to the server card (`mergeCard`, idempotent with the SSE broadcast of the same PATCH) вҶ’ reverts just that
card's stage on failure + `advanceError`. **Fallback poll** (`use-print-stream`): re-GET every 15s **only while SSE is down** (BLOCKER-B / open-q #4 вҖ” degrades
to effectively poll-only if the tunnel buffers SSE; visibility-paused; also the only path that surfaces newly-created jobs SSE doesn't emit). **Did NOT port
`use-order-poll`** (plan В§5 "reuse") вҖ” it's storefront-coupled + single-order-until-terminal semantics; the board fallback is a whole-list refresh, ~12 lines,
not a new poller. **reduced-motion** вҶ’ drop-animation off. **Filament "thiбәҝu nhб»ұa" badge DEFERRED to P3-s** (no DTO field вҖ” render no warning we can't
substantiate, not a fake placeholder). empty/loading/error all present. **Files: 11** (`print-queue.ts` pure adapters `groupByStage`/`nextStage`/`mergeCard` +

**вҖ” P3-g history (MERGED #69 вҶ’ `main` `9241ad0`) вҖ”**
**рҹ”Ё PHASE 3 В· P3-g (BE SSE `GET /admin/print-queue/stream` вҖ” live print board) вҖ” BUILT + VERIFIED on `feat/phase-3-admin-p3g-print-stream`**
(off `main` `fddfe40` after P3-f #68 merged + local main ff'd). **BE-only** (Track B, `dependsOn: P3-f`) вҖ” the live push behind the P3-h kanban so a
drag on one board reflects on every open board without polling. **KEY DESIGN вҖ” in-process hub, NOT NATS (ponytail + ADR-009):** core-api is
single-instance, so the PATCH that moves a card and every SSE subscriber are the same process вҶ’ a mutex-guarded in-process `printStreamHub`
(subscribe/broadcast/unsubscribe) suffices and is correct. ADR-008 only forbids **exposing NATS to the browser**; it does NOT mandate NATS as the
internal source. Print-stage sync is ephemeral + re-derivable (client re-GETs on reconnect) вҶ’ **no outbox, no NATS publish, no durability** (event-outbox
skill N/A). `ponytail:` if core-api ever scales horizontally, back the hub with a NATS-subscribe (SSE transport to browser unchanged). **RAW chi route,
NOT OpenAPI:** the oapi strict layer buffers the whole response вҶ’ cannot stream; `/healthz`+`/readyz` are already raw routes outside the contract
(precedent) вҶ’ **no openapi/codegen change**. Auth is **manual in-handler** via the same `resolveActor` (owner AND staff вҖ” same gate as GET
/admin/print-queue; EventSource sends `lumin_session` same-origin; no-cookie вҶ’ 401 before any stream byte). **ROUTER restructure (the crux):**
`middleware.Timeout(30s)` moved from global `r.Use` into a **Group wrapping the OpenAPI routes**, so the SSE route escapes the 30s cooperative
context-cancel; there is **no global WriteTimeout** either (main.go left it unset **deliberately** вҖ” "SSE routes need per-route handling"). **SSE
hardening (ADR-008 / conventions В§Realtime):** `text/event-stream` + `no-transform` + `Content-Encoding: identity` + `X-Accel-Buffering: no` +
`http.Flusher` per frame + **heartbeat `: ping` every 25s** (< Cloudflare 100s idle cap) + opening `: ok` comment; `event: stage` + one-line JSON `data:`
per advanced card; `r.Context().Done()` (clean, since outside Timeout) вҶ’ unsubscribe. **Broadcast** wired into `AdvancePrintJobStage` **post-commit**
(best-effort В· non-blocking В· drop-on-full вҶ’ self-heals via client GET/poll В· nil-safe). **Files: 8** (`print_stream.go` hub+handler+writeSSEEvent NEW В·
`server.go` +printHub field/init В· `admin_print_queue.go` +broadcast В· `router.go` Group+raw-route В· `middleware_auth_test.go` +printHub in
`serverWithUsers` В· `print_stream_test.go` NEW [hub fan-out В· never-blocks В· nil-safe В· auth-401 В· SSE-headers В· writeSSEEvent] В· integration
+broadcast-on-PATCH assert В· acceptance **Cб»Ҙm 32 `ADM-09`**). **Verify:** `make verify-go` вң“ (gofmt В· vet В· golangci **0** В· sqlc vet/diff В· **oapi
stale-check clean вҖ” no codegen** В· `go test -race ./...` all ok incl real-PG broadcast-on-PATCH; httpapi 43s/db 54s w/ `TESTCONTAINERS_RYUK_DISABLED=true`)
В· core `acceptance.ledger` **62** green (new `[ ]` `ADM-09`) В· `pnpm verify` **N/A** (zero TS/openapi/packages touched). **No new dep В· no new ADR**
(ADR-008 + ADR-009 cover it) **В· no migration В· no contract-break.** **вҡ пёҸ BLOCKER-B STILL OPEN вҖ” named-tunnel smoke-test is a MANUAL gate** (can't run
cloudflared here): SSE through the home-box tunnel must be smoke-tested (buffer / 100s / 524) before P3-h ships; if flaky вҶ’ **poll-only v1** (open-q #4,
ADR-008 allows; fallback `use-order-poll` P1-o already exists). **NEXT after P3-g land = P3-h** (FE `/hang-doi-in` kanban @dnd-kit + consume this SSE +
fallback poll). **Adversarial self-check + spec-guardian вҶ’ then commit вҶ’ user gate.**

any-length digit string but a napas BIN is EXACTLY 6 digits вҶ’ a fat-fingered/nonexistent numeric BIN would be stored вҶ’ misrouting
QR вҶ’ FIXED (`cleanBankUpdate` now `len(bin)==6`+digits, accountNumber digits вүӨ19 + boundary tests); (NOTE) handler validated body
[400] before owner re-assert [403] вҶ’ FIXED (authz-FIRST reorder вҖ” no per-field leak in the classify-regress path); (NOTE)
append-only untested вҶ’ REFUTED (PR-2g `db.TestBankAuditAppendOnly` already covers UPDATE/DELETE/TRUNCATE-blocked).** The owner-only
config surface the data layer deferred "to slice-3 RBAC". `internal/httpapi/settings.go`: **GetSettings** (admin-gated read,
jsonbвҶ’typed DTO, missing-singletonвҶ’logged 500 not 404) + **UpdateBankAccount** (PATCH bank-account, owner-only) +
**ListReplyTemplates**. Money-out STK change (authz FIRST): `actorFrom`вҶ’401 if absent вҶ’ **owner re-assert** (`actor.Role !=
order.RoleOwner вҶ’ 403` defense-in-depth: classify()вҶ’authOwnerOnly gates б»ҹ biГӘn, but STK is the single highest-value money-out field
so the handler re-asserts вҖ” a classify() regress can neither let staff rewrite it NOR leak field-shape detail) вҶ’ `cleanBankUpdate`
field-shape validate (**bin Д‘Гәng 6 napas digits**, accountNumber digits вүӨ19, accountName non-empty вҶ’ 400 per-field loud-reject) вҶ’
`changedBy` from **actor ctx (users.id), never body** вҶ’ `withTx` + **`db.UpdateBankAccountTx`** (column +
setting_bank_audit row **one tx**, audit-on-commit вҖ” conventions В§57). **Prior session left 3 duplicate stubs in `stubs.go`
(compile blocker) вҶ’ removed (GetDashboard/3i the last stub).** No openapi/sqlc change (contract authored in 3c-1; DTOs/req-objects
already generated) вҶ’ oapi+sqlc stale-checks clean. **guard 152вҶ’153** (+1 settings ARM PROVEN binding Г—3: `UpdateBankAccountTx` +
`order.RoleOwner` + `actorFrom` вҖ” each mutateвҶ’152/1вҶ’restore). **`STK-01`** вҶ’ acceptance Cб»Ҙm 11 (Go-gated `[ ]`). **No new deps В·
no new ADR** (impl conventions В§57/ADR-012/domain-core RBAC). Tests: 4 Docker-free unit (`TestCleanBankUpdate` field-shape В·
`TestUpdateBankAccountRejectsNonOwner` staffвҶ’403 В· `TestSettingsDTODecodesJSONB`/`EmptyJSONB` В· `TestReplyTemplatesDTO`) + 3 httpapi
integration RAN vs real PG (colima, -race): `TestUpdateBankAccountEndToEnd` (column+audit atomic, changed_by from ctx, GetSettings
reflects) В· `TestGetSettingsSeededDefaults` В· `TestListReplyTemplatesEndToEnd` (ORDER BY title). colima was ALREADY running (prior
session) вҖ” used as-is, left running.
